# Searching Sourcegraph

Search before you build. Existing patterns reduce tokens, ensure consistency, and surface tested solutions.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Tool Selection Logic

**Start here:**

1. **Know the exact symbol or pattern?** → `sg_keyword_search`
2. **Know the concept, not the code?** → `sg_nls_search`
3. **Need to understand how/why?** → `sg_deepsearch_read`
4. **Tracing a symbol's usage?** → `sg_find_references`
5. **Need full implementation?** → `sg_go_to_definition` → `sg_read_file`

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Exact code patterns | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Trace usage | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Understand systems | `sg_deepsearch_read` |
| Read files | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
file:.*\.test\.ts$ -file:__mocks__   # Tests, exclude mocks
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

Combine filters: `repo:^github.com/myorg/backend$ file:src/handlers lang:typescript`

## Context-Aware Behaviour

**When the user provides a file path or error message:**
- Extract symbols, function names, or error codes
- Search for those exact terms first
- Trace references if the error involves a known symbol

**When the user asks "how does X work":**
- Prefer `sg_deepsearch_read` for architectural understanding
- Follow up with `sg_read_file` on key files mentioned in the response

**When the user is implementing a new feature:**
- Search for similar existing implementations first
- Read tests for usage examples
- Check for shared utilities before creating new ones

**When debugging:**
- Search for the exact error string
- Trace the symbol where the error is thrown
- Check recent changes with `sg_diff_search`

## Workflows

For detailed step-by-step workflows, see:
- `workflows/implementing-feature.md` — when building new features
- `workflows/understanding-code.md` — when exploring unfamiliar systems
- `workflows/debugging-issue.md` — when tracking down bugs

## Efficiency Rules

**Minimise tool calls:**
- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms (faster, more precise)

**Batch your understanding:**
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than reading one and asking questions
- Use `sg_deepsearch_read` for "how does X work" instead of multiple keyword searches

**Avoid common token waste:**
- Don't search all repos when you know the target repo
- Don't use `sg_deepsearch_read` for simple "find all" queries
- Don't re-read files you've already seen in this conversation

## Query Patterns

| Intent | Query |
|--------|-------|
| React hooks | `file:.*\.tsx$ use[A-Z].*= \(` |
| API routes | `file:src/api app\.(get\|post\|put\|delete)` |
| Error handling | `catch.*Error\|\.catch\(` |
| Type definitions | `file:types/ export (interface\|type)` |
| Test setup | `file:.*\.test\. beforeEach\|beforeAll` |
| Config files | `file:(webpack\|vite\|rollup)\.config` |
| CI/CD | `file:\.github/workflows deploy` |

For more patterns, see `query-patterns.md`.

## Output Formatting

**Search results:**
- Present as a brief summary, not raw tool output
- Highlight the most relevant file and line
- Include a code snippet only if it directly answers the question

**Code explanations:**
- Start with a one-sentence summary
- Use the codebase's own terminology
- Reference specific files and functions

**Recommendations:**
- Present as numbered steps if actionable
- Link to specific patterns found in the codebase
- Note any existing utilities that should be reused

## Common Mistakes

| Mistake | Fix |
|---------|-----|
| Searching all repos | Add `repo:^github.com/org/repo$` |
| Too many results | Add `file:` pattern or keywords |
| Missing relevant code | Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching |
| Not understanding context | Use `sg_deepsearch_read` |
| Guessing patterns | Read implementations with `sg_read_file` |

## Principles

- Start narrow, expand if needed
- Chain tools: search → read → find references → definition
- Check tests for usage examples
- Read before generating

# Architecture Document: Envoy HTTP Connection Manager

**Repository:** envoyproxy/envoy
**Output:** Write your document to `/workspace/documentation.md`

## Task

Produce an architecture document for Envoy's **HTTP Connection Manager** (HCM) subsystem. The document must explain how the major components interact to process an HTTP request from arrival on a downstream connection through to upstream dispatch. Do not simply list APIs — explain the **design**, **data flow**, and **extension points**.

## Scope

Your document must cover these four components and how they work together:

### 1. ConnectionManagerImpl
The central network filter that owns the connection lifecycle. Explain:
- How it implements `Network::ReadFilter` to receive raw bytes
- How it creates and manages `ActiveStream` objects for each HTTP request
- Its role in codec creation (lazy codec instantiation for H1/H2 vs. H3)
- Connection-level concerns: drain decisions, overload management, watermark-based flow control

### 2. FilterManager and the HTTP Filter Chain
The per-stream filter chain execution engine. Explain:
- The decoder filter chain (request path) and encoder filter chain (response path)
- How `FilterChainFactory` creates filters for each stream
- Filter iteration: how `decodeHeaders`/`decodeData`/`decodeTrailers` propagate through decoder filters
- How filters can stop iteration, modify headers, or send local replies
- The distinction between `StreamDecoderFilter`, `StreamEncoderFilter`, and `StreamFilter` (dual)

### 3. Router Filter
The terminal decoder filter that forwards requests upstream. Explain:
- Route selection: how the router uses `RouteConfiguration` to pick a cluster
- How it obtains an HTTP connection pool from `ClusterManager`
- Upstream request lifecycle: `UpstreamRequest` creation, retry logic, timeout handling
- Shadow routing and hedged request support (if applicable)

### 4. Cluster Manager and Upstream Connectivity
The upstream connection pool and cluster management layer. Explain:
- How `ClusterManagerImpl` provides connection pools per cluster
- Load balancing: how the router obtains a host from the cluster's load balancer
- Connection pool mechanics: the relationship between logical connection pools and physical connections
- How health checking and outlier detection feed back into the load balancer

## Document Requirements

1. **Component Responsibilities** — what each component owns
2. **Data Flow** — the path of an HTTP request from downstream bytes to upstream dispatch, and the response path back
3. **Extension Points** — where users extend Envoy (HTTP filters, cluster extensions, load balancers, access loggers)
4. **Error Handling** — how errors at each stage (codec errors, filter errors, upstream failures) are handled
5. **relevant source files** — reference the actual source files in the envoyproxy/envoy repository

## Anti-Requirements

- Do NOT generate a simple API listing or header-file dump
- Do NOT fabricate class names or file paths that don't exist in the repository
- Do NOT cover Envoy components outside the HCM request path (e.g., xDS config delivery, listener management)

54-assistanttext-
The architecture document has been written to `/workspace/documentation.md`. Here is a summary of what it covers:

---

**Document structure:**

1. **ConnectionManagerImpl** — How it implements `Network::ReadFilter` to receive raw bytes, lazy codec creation for H1/H2 vs. eager for H3, the `ActiveStream` struct that owns per-request state (headers, timers, filter manager, route cache), and connection-level concerns: drain sequencing, overload management, and watermark-based flow control including the `MaxRequestsPerIoCycle` deferred-dispatch mechanism.

2. **FilterManager and HTTP Filter Chain** — How `FilterChainHelper` processes the proto filter list at config time into `FilterFactoriesList`, and how `createDownstreamFilterChain()` instantiates per-stream filter wrappers. The `StreamDecoderFilters` (forward iteration A→B→C) and `StreamEncoderFilters` (reverse iteration C→B→A) data structures. The `IterationState` enum (`Continue`, `StopSingleIteration`, `StopAllBuffer`, `StopAllWatermark`). How `sendLocalReply` either routes through the encoder chain or bypasses it with `sendDirectLocalReply`.

3. **Router Filter** — How `decodeHeaders` drives route lookup (via the `RouteCache` in `ActiveStream`), cluster resolution, `chooseHost` with synchronous and async paths, and `UpstreamRequest` creation. The `UpstreamFilterManager` / `UpstreamCodecFilter` architecture. Retry logic via `RetryStateImpl`. Hedged requests. Timeout computation. Shadow routing via `ShadowWriter`.

4. **Cluster Manager and Upstream Connectivity** — The main-thread `ClusterManagerImpl` vs. per-worker `ThreadLocalClusterManagerImpl`. Lazy cluster inflation via `ClusterInitializationObject`. Load balancer types and how the router supplies `LoadBalancerContext`. `HttpConnPoolImplBase` mechanics (pending qu
... (truncated)

{
  "content": "# Envoy HTTP Connection Manager: Architecture and Data Flow\n\n## Overview\n\nThe HTTP Connection Manager (HCM) is Envoy's central HTTP processing engine. It is a `Network::ReadFilter` that sits inside the listener filter chain and transforms a raw TCP/TLS/QUIC byte stream into structured HTTP request/response lifecycles. Four major subsystems collaborate to service every request:\n\n1. **`ConnectionManagerImpl`** \u2014 owns the connection lifecycle and codec, multiplexes raw bytes into per-request `ActiveStream` objects.\n2. **`FilterManager` / `DownstreamFilterManager`** \u2014 owns per-stream decoder and encoder filter chains, drives filter iteration.\n3. **`Router::Filter`** \u2014 the terminal decoder filter; owns route selection, upstream connection, retry, and shadow logic.\n4. **`ClusterManagerImpl` / `ThreadLocalClusterManagerImpl`** \u2014 owns upstream cluster state, load balancing, and connection pools.\n\n---\n\n## 1. ConnectionManagerImpl\n\n**Source**: `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h`, `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.cc`\n\n### Role\n\n`ConnectionManagerImpl` implements three interfaces simultaneously:\n\n- `Network::ReadFilter` \u2014 receives raw bytes from the transport layer.\n- `Http::ServerConnectionCallbacks` \u2014 called by the codec when a new HTTP stream is parsed.\n- `Network::ConnectionCallbacks` \u2014 receives connection-level events (close, watermarks).\n\nIt is instantiated per downstream TCP connection by the HCM network filter factory. The configuration comes from `ConnectionManagerConfig` (`source/common/http/conn_manager_config.h`), which exposes codec factory methods, timeout values, the filter chain factory, route provider, tracer, and access loggers.\n\n### Codec Instantiation (Lazy for H1/H2, Eager for H3)\n\nThe codec is created lazily:\n\n- For **HTTP/1 and HTTP/2**, `onData()` is the first call that receives bytes. If `codec_` is null, `createCodec()` is called immediately before dispatching:\n\n```cpp\n// conn_manager_impl.cc:505\nNetwork::FilterStatus ConnectionManagerImpl::onData(Buffer::Instance& data, bool) {\n  if (!codec_) {\n    createCodec(data);   // delegates to config_->createCodec(...)\n  }\n  const Status status = codec_->dispatch(data);\n  ...\n}\n```\n\n`createCodec()` calls `config_->createCodec()`, which inspects the first bytes (ALPN, HTTP/2 preface, etc.) to select the right `ServerConnection` implementation.\n\n- For **HTTP/3 (QUIC)**, the codec is created eagerly in `onNewConnection()` because QUICHE handles de-multiplexing at a lower level and `onData()` is never invoked.\n\nAn overload check is applied before codec creation: if the `hcm_ondata_creating_codec_` load-shed point says to shed load, the connection is closed before creating the codec.\n\n### ActiveStream: Per-Request State\n\nWhen the codec parses a new HTTP stream, it calls `ConnectionManagerImpl::newStream()`, which allocates an `ActiveStream` and puts it at the head of `streams_` (a `std::list<ActiveStreamPtr>`):\n\n```cpp\n// conn_manager_impl.cc:400\nRequestDecoder& ConnectionManagerImpl::newStream(ResponseEncoder& response_encoder, ...) {\n  auto new_stream = std::make_unique<ActiveStream>(\n      *this, response_encoder.getStream().bufferLimit(), downstream_stream_account);\n  ...\n  LinkedList::moveIntoList(std::move(new_stream), streams_);\n  return **streams_.begin();\n}\n```\n\n`ActiveStream` is a nested struct that implements multiple interfaces:\n\n| Interface | Purpose |\n|---|---|\n| `RequestDecoder` | Receives `decodeHeaders`, `decodeData`, `decodeTrailers` from the codec |\n| `FilterManagerCallbacks` | Receives encode callbacks from `DownstreamFilterManager` to write to the `ResponseEncoder` |\n| `DownstreamStreamFilterCallbacks` | Route cache management (set/clear/refresh route) |\n| `RouteCache` | Stores the snapped `RouteConfiguration` and cached `Route` |\n| `StreamCallbacks` | Receives reset and watermark events from the codec stream |\n| `ScopeTrackedObject` | Enables Envoy's crash-dump infrastructure |\n\n`ActiveStream` owns:\n- `DownstreamFilterManager filter_manager_` \u2014 the per-stream filter chain engine.\n- `RequestHeaderMapSharedPtr request_headers_`, `ResponseHeaderMapSharedPtr response_headers_`, etc.\n- Per-stream timers: `stream_idle_timer_`, `request_timer_`, `request_header_timer_`, `max_stream_duration_timer_`, `access_log_flush_timer_`.\n- `absl::optional<Router::RouteConstSharedPtr> cached_route_` \u2014 route cache with block-on-finalize semantics.\n\n### Connection-Level Concerns\n\n**Drain decisions**: `ConnectionManagerImpl` holds a `DrainState` enum (`NotDraining`, `Draining`, `Closing`). Drain is triggered by:\n- The `Network::DrainDecision` interface (server draining),\n- `maxRequestsPerConnection` threshold being reached,\n- Excessive premature RST_STREAMs (DoS protection).\n\nFor HTTP/2 and HTTP/3, drain sends a GOAWAY then waits for in-flight streams to finish. For HTTP/1, the connection is marked closing after the current stream completes.\n\n**Overload management**: Two `OverloadActionState` references are cached at construction time for the hot path:\n- `overload_stop_accepting_requests_ref_` \u2014 stops creating new streams.\n- `overload_disable_keepalive_ref_` \u2014 disables keep-alive.\n\nTwo `Server::LoadShedPoint` references control codec creation (`hcm_ondata_creating_codec_`) and header decode (`accept_new_http_stream_`).\n\n**Watermark-based flow control**: When the downstream write buffer goes above the high watermark, `onAboveWriteBufferHighWatermark()` calls `codec_->onUnderlyingConnectionAboveWriteBufferHighWatermark()`, which propagates into the active HTTP/2 or HTTP/3 codec to pause new streams. The `DownstreamFilterManager` relays the same signal into the filter chain, eventually reaching the router filter which calls `readDisable` on the upstream stream.\n\n**Per-request I/O deferral**: With the `MaxRequestsPerIoCycle` runtime flag, HCM limits the number of requests decoded in a single `onData()` invocation. Excess requests are pushed onto a `SchedulableCallback` (`deferred_request_processing_callback_`) and processed in the next event loop iteration, preventing a single connection from starving other work.\n\n---\n\n## 2. FilterManager and the HTTP Filter Chain\n\n**Source**: `source/common/http/filter_manager.h`, `source/common/http/filter_manager.cc`, `source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h`\n\n### Role\n\n`FilterManager` (base class) manages per-stream filter chain execution. `DownstreamFilterManager` (subclass) adds:\n- `StreamInfoImpl` ownership (stream info, timings, etc.).\n- Local reply logic (passing synthetic responses back through the encoder chain).\n- Load-shed integration (`downstream_filter_load_shed_point_`).\n\n### Filter Chain Data Structures\n\nTwo separate collections drive the two directions of processing:\n\n```cpp\nstruct StreamDecoderFilters {\n  std::vector<ActiveStreamDecoderFilterPtr> entries_;\n  Iterator begin() { return entries_.begin(); }  // forward: A \u2192 B \u2192 C\n};\n\nstruct StreamEncoderFilters {\n  std::vector<ActiveStreamEncoderFilterPtr> entries_;\n  Iterator begin() { return entries_.rbegin(); } // reverse: C \u2192 B \u2192 A\n};\n```\n\nEncoder filters iterate in **reverse** order of configuration, so the filter closest to the upstream (typically the router filter) encodes first, and the filter closest to the downstream encodes last.\n\nEvery filter is wrapped by either `ActiveStreamDecoderFilter` or `ActiveStreamEncoderFilter` (both extend `ActiveStreamFilterBase`). A dual filter implementing `StreamFilter` gets entries in both collections pointing to the same underlying object.\n\n### Filter Chain Creation\n\n`FilterChainHelper` (`source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h`) processes the protobuf `HttpFilter` list at config time, calling each filter's factory to produce a `FilterFactoryCb`. These callbacks are stored in `FilterFactoriesList`.\n\nAt request time, `DownstreamFilterManager::createDownstreamFilterChain()` calls `FilterChainFactory::createFilterChain()`, which iterates `FilterFactoriesList` and calls each `FilterFactoryCb` with a `FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl`. The callbacks implement `addStreamDecoderFilter`, `addStreamEncoderFilter`, and `addStreamFilter`:\n\n```cpp\n// filter_manager.h:986\nvoid addStreamDecoderFilter(StreamDecoderFilterSharedPtr filter) override {\n  manager_.decoder_filters_.entries_.emplace_back(\n      std::make_unique<ActiveStreamDecoderFilter>(manager_, std::move(filter), name));\n}\nvoid addStreamEncoderFilter(StreamEncoderFilterSharedPtr filter) override {\n  manager_.encoder_filters_.entries_.emplace_back(\n      std::make_unique<ActiveStreamEncoderFilter>(manager_, std::move(filter), name));\n}\nvoid addStreamFilter(StreamFilterSharedPtr filter) override {\n  // Adds the same object to both collections\n  manager_.decoder_filters_.entries_.emplace_back(...);\n  manager_.encoder_filters_.entries_.emplace_back(...);\n}\n```\n\nFilters can be selectively disabled per-route via `filterDisabled()` on the route.\n\n### Decoder Filter Iteration (Request Path)\n\nWhen `ActiveStream::decodeHeaders()` is called by the codec, it calls `filter_manager_.decodeHeaders(headers, end_stream)`, which invokes the private `FilterManager::decodeHeaders(nullptr, headers, end_stream)`. This iterates the decoder filter chain starting from the beginning:\n\n```\nfor each ActiveStreamDecoderFilter in decoder_filters_:\n    status = filter.decodeHeaders(headers, end_stream)\n    if status == StopIteration or StopAllIterationAndBuffer:\n        pause iteration; buffer pending data\n        return\n    // else Continue: advance to next filter\n```\n\nThe `IterationState` enum inside `ActiveStreamFilterBase` tracks the current state per filter:\n- `Continue` \u2014 iteration is active.\n- `StopSingleIteration` \u2014 paused for this frame type only; headers done but data/trailers will still iterate.\n- `StopAllBuffer` \u2014 all frame types are paused and buffered.\n- `StopAllWatermark` \u2014 buffered until the high watermark is reached, then pushes back to downstream.\n\nWhen a filter calls `continueDecoding()`, `commonContinue()` resumes iteration starting from the filter that stopped it (`iterate_from_current_filter_` flag), then advances to subsequent filters.\n\nThe same pattern applies to `decodeData` and `decodeTrailers`.\n\n### Encoder Filter Iteration (Response Path)\n\nThe upstream response arrives (via the router filter) as a call to `ActiveStreamDecoderFilter::encodeHeaders()`, which routes into `FilterManager::encodeHeaders()`. This iterates `encoder_filters_` **in reverse** (C \u2192 B \u2192 A), allowing filters closer to the downstream to be the last to modify the response before it is written to the `ResponseEncoder`.\n\nAfter all encoder filters complete, `FilterManagerCallbacks::encodeHeaders()` (implemented by `ActiveStream`) writes the final headers to the codec's `ResponseEncoder`, emitting bytes onto the downstream connection.\n\n### Local Replies\n\nA filter may call `sendLocalReply()` from anywhere in the decoder chain. `DownstreamFilterManager::sendLocalReply()` implements two strategies:\n\n1. **Via filter chain** (`sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain` / `prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain`): constructs a synthetic response and runs it through all encoder filters, giving encoder filters a chance to transform the error response.\n2. **Direct** (`sendDirectLocalReply`): bypasses the encoder chain and writes directly to the `ResponseEncoder`. Used for streaming scenarios or when the encoder chain has already been walked.\n\nPrepared local replies are stored in `prepared_local_reply_` and executed via `executeLocalReplyIfPrepared()` after the current decoder filter call returns, preventing re-entrant filter iteration.\n\n---\n\n## 3. Router Filter\n\n**Source**: `source/common/router/router.h`, `source/common/router/router.cc`, `source/common/router/upstream_request.h`\n\n### Role\n\n`Router::Filter` is the terminal `StreamDecoderFilter` in the downstream filter chain. It owns:\n- Route selection.\n- Upstream connection pool acquisition.\n- `UpstreamRequest` creation and retry management.\n- Shadow routing.\n- Timeout management.\n- Upstream filter chain (via `UpstreamFilterManager`).\n\n`Router::Filter` also implements `Upstream::LoadBalancerContextBase`, providing hash keys, metadata match criteria, and host selection constraints to the load balancer.\n\n### Route Selection\n\n`decodeHeaders()` is the entry point. The route is obtained from the cached route in `ActiveStream` via `callbacks_->route()`:\n\n```cpp\n// router.cc:471\nroute_ = callbacks_->route();\nif (!route_) {\n    callbacks_->sendLocalReply(Http::Code::NotFound, ...);\n    return StopIteration;\n}\n```\n\nThe `ActiveStream` implements `RouteCache`. It lazily calls `ConnectionManagerConfig::routeConfigProvider()` (for static/RDS routes) or `scopedRouteConfigProvider()` (for scoped routing), matches the request headers against the `RouteConfiguration`, and caches the result. The route cache is **blocked** (frozen) at the point response headers are processed, preventing route mutations during the response path.\n\nRoute matching is done by `Router::ConfigImpl::route()` (`source/common/router/config_impl.cc`), which walks virtual hosts, then route entries (prefix, path, regex), and evaluates route matchers (headers, query params, runtime fractions).\n\nOnce a route entry is selected:\n- `route_entry_->clusterName()` (or a `ClusterSpecifierPlugin`) identifies the target cluster.\n- `config_->cm_.getThreadLocalCluster(name)` obtains the thread-local cluster object (or null if not found \u2192 503).\n\n### Host Selection and Connection Pool Acquisition\n\nAfter the cluster is identified, the router selects a host and creates a connection pool handle:\n\n```cpp\n// router.cc:700\nauto host_selection_response = cluster->chooseHost(this);\n// ...\nstd::unique_ptr<GenericConnPool> generic_conn_pool = createConnPool(*cluster, selected_host);\n```\n\n`chooseHost()` delegates to the cluster's `LoadBalancer` (inside `ClusterEntry`). If asynchronous host selection is enabled (e.g., on-demand CDS), `chooseHost` returns a cancellable handle and a callback is registered; filter chain iteration returns `StopAllIterationAndWatermark` until the async callback fires.\n\n`createConnPool()` calls `cluster->httpConnPool(host, priority, downstream_protocol, this)`, which returns a `GenericConnPool` wrapping the appropriate `Http::ConnectionPool::Instance`. The connection pool is keyed by (host, priority, protocol) in the thread-local `host_http_conn_pool_map_`.\n\n### UpstreamRequest Lifecycle\n\nFor each attempt (initial + retries), the router creates an `UpstreamRequest`:\n\n```cpp\n// router.cc:842\nUpstreamRequestPtr upstream_request = std::make_unique<UpstreamRequest>(\n    *this, std::move(generic_conn_pool), can_send_early_data, can_use_http3, enable_half_close);\nLinkedList::moveIntoList(std::move(upstream_request), upstream_requests_);\nupstream_requests_.front()->acceptHeadersFromRouter(end_stream);\n```\n\n`UpstreamRequest` owns an **upstream filter chain** via `UpstreamFilterManager` and `UpstreamRequestFilterManagerCallbacks`. Request data arriving via `acceptHeadersFromRouter`, `acceptDataFromRouter`, `acceptTrailersFromRouter` is passed into this upstream filter manager. The last filter in the upstream chain is always `UpstreamCodecFilter` (`source/common/router/upstream_codec_filter.cc`), which holds the actual stream on the upstream connection.\n\nWhen the upstream connection is not yet ready, `UpstreamCodecFilter` returns `StopAllIteration`, causing the upstream filter manager to buffer the request and use watermarks to push back on the router (and in turn the downstream) if buffers fill up.\n\nOn `onPoolReady` (connection established, stream allocated):\n1. The `UpstreamRequest` obtains a `GenericUpstream` handle.\n2. `UpstreamCodecFilter` encodes the buffered request headers/data.\n\nOn `onPoolFailure` (no healthy hosts, connection error, etc.):\n1. `UpstreamRequest::onPoolFailure()` calls `parent_.onUpstreamAbort()`.\n2. The router checks the retry policy; if retriable, it calls `doRetry()`.\n3. If no more retries, `sendLocalReply` is called with a 503 or 504.\n\n### Retry Logic\n\n`RetryStateImpl` (`source/common/router/retry_state_impl.cc`) evaluates whether a response or reset event is retriable:\n- HTTP status codes (5xx, specific codes).\n- Reset reasons (connection failure, refused-stream).\n- Per-try timeouts with hedging.\n\nOn a retriable failure, `doRetry()` creates a new `UpstreamRequest`, either immediately or after the previous one is fully cleaned up. Retry attempt count and headers (`x-envoy-attempt-count`) are updated on the downstream request before each retry.\n\nHedged requests (configured via `hedge_on_per_try_timeout`) keep the original upstream request alive while launching a new one; when either returns a valid response, the winning response is forwarded downstream and the other upstream request is reset.\n\n### Timeout Handling\n\n`FilterUtility::finalTimeout()` computes two timeout values:\n- **Global timeout**: overall deadline for the entire request including retries.\n- **Per-try timeout**: deadline for each individual upstream attempt.\n\nThe global timeout fires via `response_timeout_` (`Event::TimerPtr`), calling `onGlobalTimeout()` \u2192 `sendLocalReply(504)`. Per-try timeout fires via `UpstreamRequest::per_try_timeout_`, calling `onPerTryTimeout()` which triggers a retry if configured.\n\n### Shadow Routing\n\nShadow (traffic mirroring) is evaluated per route and per cluster `shadowPolicies()`. For each active shadow policy, the router copies the request headers, optionally modifies them (cluster name override, weight-based sampling), and sends to the shadow cluster via `config_->shadowWriter().shadow()`, which uses `Http::AsyncClient` so the shadow stream does not affect the downstream response.\n\n---\n\n## 4. Cluster Manager and Upstream Connectivity\n\n**Source**: `source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.h`, `source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.cc`, `source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.h`, `source/common/http/conn_pool_base.h`\n\n### ClusterManagerImpl\n\n`ClusterManagerImpl` is a singleton (one per Envoy server) that maintains the canonical list of active and warming clusters. Each cluster is represented by a `ClusterData` object holding:\n- `Cluster` \u2014 the cluster implementation (static/EDS/DNS/logical DNS/original dst).\n- `ThreadAwareLoadBalancer` \u2014 if present, a thread-aware LB (e.g., ring hash, maglev); otherwise each thread gets its own independent LB.\n\nCluster updates from CDS flow through `addOrUpdateCluster()`, which updates the main-thread state and then posts to each worker thread via `postThreadLocalClusterUpdate()`.\n\n### ThreadLocalClusterManagerImpl\n\nEach worker thread has a `ThreadLocalClusterManagerImpl` (stored in thread-local storage via `ThreadLocal::Slot`). It holds:\n\n```cpp\nabsl::flat_hash_map<std::string, ClusterEntryPtr> thread_local_clusters_;\nabsl::node_hash_map<HostConstSharedPtr, ConnPoolsContainer> host_http_conn_pool_map_;\n```\n\n`ClusterEntry` (inner class of `ThreadLocalClusterManagerImpl`) implements `ThreadLocalCluster` and owns:\n- `PrioritySetImpl priority_set_` \u2014 the local view of healthy/degraded hosts at each priority level.\n- `LoadBalancerPtr lb_` \u2014 the thread-local load balancer instance.\n\n**Lazy cluster inflation**: With the `ClusterInitializationObject` mechanism, worker threads can defer constructing a `ClusterEntry` until the first request arrives for that cluster (`initializeClusterInlineIfExists`). This reduces memory pressure for clusters that are rarely used on a given thread.\n\n### Load Balancing\n\n`ThreadLocalCluster::chooseHost(LoadBalancerContext*)` calls into the `LoadBalancer` interface. The load balancer is provided by a factory from the cluster configuration:\n- **Round Robin**: iterates hosts in the priority set.\n- **Least Request**: selects the host with the fewest active requests.\n- **Ring Hash / Maglev**: consistent hashing using `computeHashKey()` from the `LoadBalancerContext` (router filter computes the hash from request headers or a cookie).\n- **Random**: uniform random selection.\n- **Custom**: via `loadBalancingPolicy` extension (e.g., `peak_ewma` in contrib).\n\nThe router filter implements `LoadBalancerContextBase` to supply:\n- `computeHashKey()` \u2014 from the `HashPolicy` configured on the route or cluster.\n- `metadataMatchCriteria()` \u2014 merged from route, connection, and request metadata for subset load balancing.\n- `shouldSelectAnotherHost()` \u2014 delegates to `RetryStateImpl` to avoid previously-failed hosts on retry.\n- `determinePriorityLoad()` \u2014 adjusts priority weights on retry.\n\n### Connection Pool Mechanics\n\n`ThreadLocalCluster::httpConnPool(host, priority, downstream_protocol, context)` returns an `HttpPoolData` wrapping the appropriate `Http::ConnectionPool::Instance`. Connection pools are stored in `host_http_conn_pool_map_` keyed by a hash of (host, priority, protocol, options).\n\n`HttpConnPoolImplBase` (`source/common/http/conn_pool_base.h`) is the base for HTTP/1.1 and HTTP/2 pools. It builds on `ConnPoolImplBase` (`source/common/conn_pool/conn_pool_base.h`), which maintains:\n- `pending_streams_` \u2014 requests waiting for a connection.\n- `ready_clients_` \u2014 clients with capacity to accept a new stream.\n- `busy_clients_` \u2014 clients at their concurrent stream limit.\n\nWhen `newStream()` is called:\n1. If a ready client exists, the stream is immediately attached.\n2. If the pool can grow (below `max_connections`), a new `CodecClient` is created (one TCP connection per client for HTTP/1.1, one per cluster host for HTTP/2 multiplexed).\n3. Otherwise, the request queues as an `HttpPendingStream`.\n\nWhen a connection becomes ready (TLS handshake complete, HTTP/2 SETTINGS exchanged), pending streams are drained from the queue. Idle pool connections are drained after `idle_timeout` with a configurable grace period.\n\nFor **HTTP/3 (QUIC)**, the `conn_pool_grid.h` (`Http::ConnectivityGrid`) implements Happy Eyeballs between H3 and H1/H2, falling back if QUIC is unavailable.\n\n### Health Checking and Outlier Detection\n\n**Active health checks** (`source/common/upstream/health_checker_impl.cc`) send periodic HTTP/TCP/gRPC probes to each host. The `HealthCheckerImpl` subscribes to each host and calls `setHealthy()/setUnhealthy()` based on probe results. These status changes are propagated through the `PrioritySet` \u2192 `LoadBalancer`, removing unhealthy hosts from the eligible set.\n\n**Outlier detection** (`source/common/upstream/outlier_detection_impl.cc`) monitors request outcomes reported by the router via `updateOutlierDetection()`:\n\n```cpp\n// router.cc - after receiving upstream response\nvoid Filter::updateOutlierDetection(Upstream::Outlier::Result result,\n                                    UpstreamRequest& upstream_request, ...) {\n    ...host->outlierDetector().putResult(result, code);\n}\n```\n\n`DetectorImpl` accumulates per-host failure counters and runs periodic analysis. When a host breaches a configured threshold (consecutive 5xx errors, local origin failures, success rate below cluster average), it is **ejected** for an exponentially-increasing interval (`base_ejection_time * consecutive_ejections`). Ejected hosts are marked `UNHEALTHY` in the host's health flags and excluded by the load balancer.\n\nHealth state is written by the main thread but read by worker threads through the `HostSharedPtr` reference-counted objects, which carry atomic health-flag bitfields updated with appropriate memory ordering.\n\n---\n\n## 5. Complete Data Flow: Request Path\n\n```\nDownstream TCP/TLS connection\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc\nConnectionManagerImpl::onData()       [Network::ReadFilter]\n  \u2514\u2500 createCodec() if first bytes      [lazy, except QUIC]\n  \u2514\u2500 codec_->dispatch(data)            [ServerConnection: H1/H2/H3 parsing]\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc codec calls ServerConnectionCallbacks\nConnectionManagerImpl::newStream()     [allocates ActiveStream]\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc codec calls RequestDecoder (ActiveStream)\nActiveStream::decodeHeaders()\n  \u2514\u2500 validates headers (UHV if enabled)\n  \u2514\u2500 filter_manager_.decodeHeaders()\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc FilterManager iterates decoder_filters_ forward\n[FilterA::decodeHeaders] \u2192 [FilterB::decodeHeaders] \u2192 [Router::Filter::decodeHeaders]\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc Router::Filter\n  \u2514\u2500 callbacks_->route()              [ActiveStream::route() \u2192 RouteConfig match]\n  \u2514\u2500 config_->cm_.getThreadLocalCluster(cluster_name)\n  \u2514\u2500 cluster->chooseHost(this)         [LoadBalancer host selection]\n  \u2514\u2500 cluster->httpConnPool(host, ...)  [Thread-local pool lookup/create]\n  \u2514\u2500 new UpstreamRequest(conn_pool)\n  \u2514\u2500 upstream_request->acceptHeadersFromRouter()\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc UpstreamRequest / UpstreamFilterManager\n  [UpstreamFilterA \u2192 UpstreamCodecFilter]\n  \u2514\u2500 conn_pool->newStream(response_decoder, callbacks)\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc ConnectionPool\n  \u2514\u2500 Existing idle connection? Attach stream immediately.\n     No? \u2192 Create new CodecClient (TCP connect + TLS + ALPN + H2 SETTINGS)\n     Queue as HttpPendingStream if at capacity.\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc onPoolReady (new or existing upstream connection)\n  \u2514\u2500 UpstreamCodecFilter encodes headers onto upstream stream\n  \u2514\u2500 Upstream data flushed\n```\n\n## 6. Complete Data Flow: Response Path\n\n```\nUpstream bytes received by CodecClient\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc UpstreamCodecFilter::CodecBridge (Http::ResponseDecoder)\n  \u2514\u2500 decode1xxHeaders / decodeHeaders / decodeData / decodeTrailers\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc UpstreamRequestFilterManagerCallbacks::encodeHeaders()\n  \u2514\u2500 upstream_request_.decodeHeaders(response_headers, end_stream)\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc UpstreamRequest::decodeHeaders()\n  \u2514\u2500 parent_.onUpstreamHeaders(status_code, headers, upstream_request, end_stream)\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc Router::Filter::onUpstreamHeaders()\n  \u2514\u2500 Check for retry: RetryStateImpl::shouldRetryHeaders()\n     If retry \u2192 doRetry() \u2192 new UpstreamRequest\n     Else \u2192 forward downstream:\n  \u2514\u2500 callbacks_->encodeHeaders(response_headers, end_stream)   [ActiveStreamDecoderFilter]\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc FilterManager::encodeHeaders() \u2014 iterates encoder_filters_ REVERSE\n[Router side-effects] \u2192 [FilterC::encodeHeaders] \u2192 [FilterB::encodeHeaders] \u2192 [FilterA::encodeHeaders]\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc FilterManagerCallbacks::encodeHeaders() [ActiveStream]\n  \u2514\u2500 response_encoder_->encodeHeaders()          [H1/H2/H3 ResponseEncoder]\n  \u2514\u2500 Bytes written to downstream connection write buffer\n  \u2514\u2500 Access logging on stream completion\n  \u2514\u2500 doDeferredStreamDestroy(stream)\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Extension Points\n\n| Extension Point | Interface / Location |\n|---|---|\n| **HTTP filters** (decoder/encoder/dual) | `Http::StreamDecoderFilter`, `Http::StreamEncoderFilter`, `Http::StreamFilter` registered via `NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory` |\n| **Upstream HTTP filters** | Same interfaces, registered via `UpstreamHttpFilterConfigFactory`, placed in `UpstreamFilterManager` |\n| **Load balancers** | `LoadBalancerFactory` / `ThreadAwareLoadBalancerFactory` (`envoy/upstream/load_balancer.h`) |\n| **Cluster types** | `ClusterFactory` (`envoy/upstream/cluster_factory.h`) |\n| **Health checkers** | `HealthCheckerFactory` (`envoy/server/health_checker_config.h`) |\n| **Outlier detectors** | `OutlierDetectionFactory` |\n| **Access loggers** | `AccessLog::InstanceFactory` (`envoy/access_log/access_log_config.h`) |\n| **Tracers** | `Tracing::Driver` factory (`envoy/server/tracer_config.h`) |\n| **Route config providers** | `RouteConfigProviderManager`, `RdsRouteConfigProviderFactory` |\n| **Cluster specifier plugins** | `ClusterSpecifierPlugin` (`envoy/router/cluster_specifier_plugin.h`) |\n| **Request ID extensions** | `RequestIDExtension` (`envoy/http/request_id_extension.h`) |\n| **Header validators** | `HeaderValidatorFactory` (`envoy/http/header_validator_factory.h`) \u2014 compile-time via `ENVOY_ENABLE_UHV` |\n| **Original IP detection** | `OriginalIPDetectionExtension` (`envoy/http/original_ip_detection.h`) |\n| **Early header mutations** | `EarlyHeaderMutation` (`envoy/http/early_header_mutation.h`) |\n| **Shadow writers** | `ShadowWriter` (`envoy/router/shadow_writer.h`) |\n\n---\n\n## 8. Error Handling\n\n### Codec Errors\n\nDetected in `ConnectionManagerImpl::onData()` after `codec_->dispatch()`. The returned `Status` is classified:\n\n- `isBufferFloodError` / `isInboundFramesWithEmptyPayloadError` \u2192 `handleCodecError()` \u2192 `doConnectionClose(FlushWriteAndDelay)`.\n- `isCodecProtocolError` \u2192 same, increments `downstream_cx_protocol_error_`.\n- `isEnvoyOverloadError` \u2192 `handleCodecOverloadError()` \u2192 same.\n\nHTTP/1 codec sends a `400 Bad Request` before closing. HTTP/2 codec sends a GOAWAY. All active streams receive an `onResetStream` callback from `resetAllStreams()`.\n\n### Filter Errors\n\n- A filter returning `StopIteration` during `decodeHeaders` after calling `sendLocalReply` initiates the local reply path. The downstream filter chain iteration is aborted (`decoder_filter_chain_aborted_ = true`). The local reply goes through encoder filters (or is sent directly if encoder chain is not applicable).\n- If a filter throws (fatal error), Envoy's crash handler terminates. Non-fatal filter errors must be handled by the filter itself using `sendLocalReply`.\n- The `MissingConfigFilter` handles the ECDS case where a dynamic filter configuration has not yet loaded, returning a 500.\n\n### Upstream Failures\n\nHandled by `Router::Filter`:\n\n| Failure Type | Handling |\n|---|---|\n| Pool failure (no healthy upstream) | `onPoolFailure()` \u2192 `onUpstreamAbort()` \u2192 retry or 503 |\n| Connection reset during request | `onUpstreamReset()` \u2192 retry if `RetryState::shouldRetryReset()` |\n| Per-try timeout | `onPerTryTimeout()` \u2192 retry with hedging if enabled |\n| Global timeout | `onGlobalTimeout()` \u2192 `sendLocalReply(504)`, all upstream requests reset |\n| Upstream 5xx response | `RetryState::shouldRetryHeaders()` \u2192 retry or forward to downstream |\n| Upstream max stream duration | `onStreamMaxDurationReached()` \u2192 reset upstream, retry or 504 |\n\nUpstream failures are also reported to outlier detection via `updateOutlierDetection()`, contributing to host ejection.\n\n### Connection-Level Failures\n\n`ConnectionManagerImpl::onEvent()` handles `Network::ConnectionEvent::RemoteClose` and `LocalClose`. It calls `resetAllStreams(CoreResponseFlag::DownstreamConnectionTermination, ...)`, which invokes `onResetStream` on every `ActiveStream`, causing the router to clean up upstream connections.\n\n---\n\n## 9. Key Source Files Reference\n\n| Component | File |\n|---|---|\n| HCM implementation | `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h`, `.cc` |\n| HCM configuration | `source/common/http/conn_manager_config.h` |\n| Filter Manager | `source/common/http/filter_manager.h`, `.cc` |\n| Filter chain construction | `source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h`, `.cc` |\n| Router filter | `source/common/router/router.h`, `.cc` |\n| Router config (route matching) | `source/common/router/config_impl.h`, `.cc` |\n| Upstream request | `source/common/router/upstream_request.h`, `.cc` |\n| Upstream codec filter | `source/common/router/upstream_codec_filter.h`, `.cc` |\n| Retry state | `source/common/router/retry_state_impl.h`, `.cc` |\n| Shadow writer | `source/common/router/shadow_writer_impl.h`, `.cc` |\n| Cluster manager | `source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.h`, `.cc` |\n| Cluster implementation | `source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.h`, `.cc` |\n| HTTP connection pool base | `source/common/http/conn_pool_base.h`, `.cc` |\n| HTTP/1 connection pool | `source/common/http/http1/` |\n| HTTP/2 connection pool | `source/common/http/http2/` |\n| H2+H3 grid pool | `source/common/http/conn_pool_grid.h`, `.cc` |\n| Health checker | `source/common/upstream/health_checker_impl.h`, `.cc` |\n| Outlier detection | `source/common/upstream/outlier_detection_impl.h`, `.cc` |\n| Public HCM filter interface | `envoy/http/filter.h` |\n| Cluster manager interface | `envoy/upstream/cluster_manager.h` |\n| Load balancer interface | `envoy/upstream/load_balancer.h` |\n",

{
  "content": "# Envoy HTTP Connection Manager: Architecture and Data Flow\n\n## Overview\n\nThe HTTP Connection Manager (HCM) is Envoy's central HTTP processing engine. It is a `Network::ReadFilter` that sits inside the listener filter chain and transforms a raw TCP/TLS/QUIC byte stream into structured HTTP request/response lifecycles. Four major subsystems collaborate to service every request:\n\n1. **`ConnectionManagerImpl`** \u2014 owns the connection lifecycle and codec, multiplexes raw bytes into per-request `ActiveStream` objects.\n2. **`FilterManager` / `DownstreamFilterManager`** \u2014 owns per-stream decoder and encoder filter chains, drives filter iteration.\n3. **`Router::Filter`** \u2014 the terminal decoder filter; owns route selection, upstream connection, retry, and shadow logic.\n4. **`ClusterManagerImpl` / `ThreadLocalClusterManagerImpl`** \u2014 owns upstream cluster state, load balancing, and connection pools.\n\n---\n\n## 1. ConnectionManagerImpl\n\n**Source**: `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h`, `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.cc`\n\n### Role\n\n`ConnectionManagerImpl` implements three interfaces simultaneously:\n\n- `Network::ReadFilter` \u2014 receives raw bytes from the transport layer.\n- `Http::ServerConnectionCallbacks` \u2014 called by the codec when a new HTTP stream is parsed.\n- `Network::ConnectionCallbacks` \u2014 receives connection-level events (close, watermarks).\n\nIt is instantiated per downstream TCP connection by the HCM network filter factory. The configuration comes from `ConnectionManagerConfig` (`source/common/http/conn_manager_config.h`), which exposes codec factory methods, timeout values, the filter chain factory, route provider, tracer, and access loggers.\n\n### Codec Instantiation (Lazy for H1/H2, Eager for H3)\n\nThe codec is created lazily:\n\n- For **HTTP/1 and HTTP/2**, `onData()` is the first call that receives bytes. If `codec_` is null, `createCodec()` is called immediately before dispatching:\n\n```cpp\n// conn_manager_impl.cc:505\nNetwork::FilterStatus ConnectionManagerImpl::onData(Buffer::Instance& data, bool) {\n  if (!codec_) {\n    createCodec(data);   // delegates to config_->createCodec(...)\n  }\n  const Status status = codec_->dispatch(data);\n  ...\n}\n```\n\n`createCodec()` calls `config_->createCodec()`, which inspects the first bytes (ALPN, HTTP/2 preface, etc.) to select the right `ServerConnection` implementation.\n\n- For **HTTP/3 (QUIC)**, the codec is created eagerly in `onNewConnection()` because QUICHE handles de-multiplexing at a lower level and `onData()` is never invoked.\n\nAn overload check is applied before codec creation: if the `hcm_ondata_creating_codec_` load-shed point says to shed load, the connection is closed before creating the codec.\n\n### ActiveStream: Per-Request State\n\nWhen the codec parses a new HTTP stream, it calls `ConnectionManagerImpl::newStream()`, which allocates an `ActiveStream` and puts it at the head of `streams_` (a `std::list<ActiveStreamPtr>`):\n\n```cpp\n// conn_manager_impl.cc:400\nRequestDecoder& ConnectionManagerImpl::newStream(ResponseEncoder& response_encoder, ...) {\n  auto new_stream = std::make_unique<ActiveStream>(\n      *this, response_encoder.getStream().bufferLimit(), downstream_stream_account);\n  ...\n  LinkedList::moveIntoList(std::move(new_stream), streams_);\n  return **streams_.begin();\n}\n```\n\n`ActiveStream` is a nested struct that implements multiple interfaces:\n\n| Interface | Purpose |\n|---|---|\n| `RequestDecoder` | Receives `decodeHeaders`, `decodeData`, `decodeTrailers` from the codec |\n| `FilterManagerCallbacks` | Receives encode callbacks from `DownstreamFilterManager` to write to the `ResponseEncoder` |\n| `DownstreamStreamFilterCallbacks` | Route cache management (set/clear/refresh route) |\n| `RouteCache` | Stores the snapped `RouteConfiguration` and cached `Route` |\n| `StreamCallbacks` | Receives reset and watermark events from the codec stream |\n| `ScopeTrackedObject` | Enables Envoy's crash-dump infrastructure |\n\n`ActiveStream` owns:\n- `DownstreamFilterManager filter_manager_` \u2014 the per-stream filter chain engine.\n- `RequestHeaderMapSharedPtr request_headers_`, `ResponseHeaderMapSharedPtr response_headers_`, etc.\n- Per-stream timers: `stream_idle_timer_`, `request_timer_`, `request_header_timer_`, `max_stream_duration_timer_`, `access_log_flush_timer_`.\n- `absl::optional<Router::RouteConstSharedPtr> cached_route_` \u2014 route cache with block-on-finalize semantics.\n\n### Connection-Level Concerns\n\n**Drain decisions**: `ConnectionManagerImpl` holds a `DrainState` enum (`NotDraining`, `Draining`, `Closing`). Drain is triggered by:\n- The `Network::DrainDecision` interface (server draining),\n- `maxRequestsPerConnection` threshold being reached,\n- Excessive premature RST_STREAMs (DoS protection).\n\nFor HTTP/2 and HTTP/3, drain sends a GOAWAY then waits for in-flight streams to finish. For HTTP/1, the connection is marked closing after the current stream completes.\n\n**Overload management**: Two `OverloadActionState` references are cached at construction time for the hot path:\n- `overload_stop_accepting_requests_ref_` \u2014 stops creating new streams.\n- `overload_disable_keepalive_ref_` \u2014 disables keep-alive.\n\nTwo `Server::LoadShedPoint` references control codec creation (`hcm_ondata_creating_codec_`) and header decode (`accept_new_http_stream_`).\n\n**Watermark-based flow control**: When the downstream write buffer goes above the high watermark, `onAboveWriteBufferHighWatermark()` calls `codec_->onUnderlyingConnectionAboveWriteBufferHighWatermark()`, which propagates into the active HTTP/2 or HTTP/3 codec to pause new streams. The `DownstreamFilterManager` relays the same signal into the filter chain, eventually reaching the router filter which calls `readDisable` on the upstream stream.\n\n**Per-request I/O deferral**: With the `MaxRequestsPerIoCycle` runtime flag, HCM limits the number of requests decoded in a single `onData()` invocation. Excess requests are pushed onto a `SchedulableCallback` (`deferred_request_processing_callback_`) and processed in the next event loop iteration, preventing a single connection from starving other work.\n\n---\n\n## 2. FilterManager and the HTTP Filter Chain\n\n**Source**: `source/common/http/filter_manager.h`, `source/common/http/filter_manager.cc`, `source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h`\n\n### Role\n\n`FilterManager` (base class) manages per-stream filter chain execution. `DownstreamFilterManager` (subclass) adds:\n- `StreamInfoImpl` ownership (stream info, timings, etc.).\n- Local reply logic (passing synthetic responses back through the encoder chain).\n- Load-shed integration (`downstream_filter_load_shed_point_`).\n\n### Filter Chain Data Structures\n\nTwo separate collections drive the two directions of processing:\n\n```cpp\nstruct StreamDecoderFilters {\n  std::vector<ActiveStreamDecoderFilterPtr> entries_;\n  Iterator begin() { return entries_.begin(); }  // forward: A \u2192 B \u2192 C\n};\n\nstruct StreamEncoderFilters {\n  std::vector<ActiveStreamEncoderFilterPtr> entries_;\n  Iterator begin() { return entries_.rbegin(); } // reverse: C \u2192 B \u2192 A\n};\n```\n\nEncoder filters iterate in **reverse** order of configuration, so the filter closest to the upstream (typically the router filter) encodes first, and the filter closest to the downstream encodes last.\n\nEvery filter is wrapped by either `ActiveStreamDecoderFilter` or `ActiveStreamEncoderFilter` (both extend `ActiveStreamFilterBase`). A dual filter implementing `StreamFilter` gets entries in both collections pointing to the same underlying object.\n\n### Filter Chain Creation\n\n`FilterChainHelper` (`source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h`) processes the protobuf `HttpFilter` list at config time, calling each filter's factory to produce a `FilterFactoryCb`. These callbacks are stored in `FilterFactoriesList`.\n\nAt request time, `DownstreamFilterManager::createDownstreamFilterChain()` calls `FilterChainFactory::createFilterChain()`, which iterates `FilterFactoriesList` and calls each `FilterFactoryCb` with a `FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl`. The callbacks implement `addStreamDecoderFilter`, `addStreamEncoderFilter`, and `addStreamFilter`:\n\n```cpp\n// filter_manager.h:986\nvoid addStreamDecoderFilter(StreamDecoderFilterSharedPtr filter) override {\n  manager_.decoder_filters_.entries_.emplace_back(\n      std::make_unique<ActiveStreamDecoderFilter>(manager_, std::move(filter), name));\n}\nvoid addStreamEncoderFilter(StreamEncoderFilterSharedPtr filter) override {\n  manager_.encoder_filters_.entries_.emplace_back(\n      std::make_unique<ActiveStreamEncoderFilter>(manager_, std::move(filter), name));\n}\nvoid addStreamFilter(StreamFilterSharedPtr filter) override {\n  // Adds the same object to both collections\n  manager_.decoder_filters_.entries_.emplace_back(...);\n  manager_.encoder_filters_.entries_.emplace_back(...);\n}\n```\n\nFilters can be selectively disabled per-route via `filterDisabled()` on the route.\n\n### Decoder Filter Iteration (Request Path)\n\nWhen `ActiveStream::decodeHeaders()` is called by the codec, it calls `filter_manager_.decodeHeaders(headers, end_stream)`, which invokes the private `FilterManager::decodeHeaders(nullptr, headers, end_stream)`. This iterates the decoder filter chain starting from the beginning:\n\n```\nfor each ActiveStreamDecoderFilter in decoder_filters_:\n    status = filter.decodeHeaders(headers, end_stream)\n    if status == StopIteration or StopAllIterationAndBuffer:\n        pause iteration; buffer pending data\n        return\n    // else Continue: advance to next filter\n```\n\nThe `IterationState` enum inside `ActiveStreamFilterBase` tracks the current state per filter:\n- `Continue` \u2014 iteration is active.\n- `StopSingleIteration` \u2014 paused for this frame type only; headers done but data/trailers will still iterate.\n- `StopAllBuffer` \u2014 all frame types are paused and buffered.\n- `StopAllWatermark` \u2014 buffered until the high watermark is reached, then pushes back to downstream.\n\nWhen a filter calls `continueDecoding()`, `commonContinue()` resumes iteration starting from the filter that stopped it (`iterate_from_current_filter_` flag), then advances to subsequent filters.\n\nThe same pattern applies to `decodeData` and `decodeTrailers`.\n\n### Encoder Filter Iteration (Response Path)\n\nThe upstream response arrives (via the router filter) as a call to `ActiveStreamDecoderFilter::encodeHeaders()`, which routes into `FilterManager::encodeHeaders()`. This iterates `encoder_filters_` **in reverse** (C \u2192 B \u2192 A), allowing filters closer to the downstream to be the last to modify the response before it is written to the `ResponseEncoder`.\n\nAfter all encoder filters complete, `FilterManagerCallbacks::encodeHeaders()` (implemented by `ActiveStream`) writes the final headers to the codec's `ResponseEncoder`, emitting bytes onto the downstream connection.\n\n### Local Replies\n\nA filter may call `sendLocalReply()` from anywhere in the decoder chain. `DownstreamFilterManager::sendLocalReply()` implements two strategies:\n\n1. **Via filter chain** (`sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain` / `prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain`): constructs a synthetic response and runs it through all encoder filters, giving encoder filters a chance to transform the error response.\n2. **Direct** (`sendDirectLocalReply`): bypasses the encoder chain and writes directly to the `ResponseEncoder`. Used for streaming scenarios or when the encoder chain has already been walked.\n\nPrepared local replies are stored in `prepared_local_reply_` and executed via `executeLocalReplyIfPrepared()` after the current decoder filter call returns, preventing re-entrant filter iteration.\n\n---\n\n## 3. Router Filter\n\n**Source**: `source/common/router/router.h`, `source/common/router/router.cc`, `source/common/router/upstream_request.h`\n\n### Role\n\n`Router::Filter` is the terminal `StreamDecoderFilter` in the downstream filter chain. It owns:\n- Route selection.\n- Upstream connection pool acquisition.\n- `UpstreamRequest` creation and retry management.\n- Shadow routing.\n- Timeout management.\n- Upstream filter chain (via `UpstreamFilterManager`).\n\n`Router::Filter` also implements `Upstream::LoadBalancerContextBase`, providing hash keys, metadata match criteria, and host selection constraints to the load balancer.\n\n### Route Selection\n\n`decodeHeaders()` is the entry point. The route is obtained from the cached route in `ActiveStream` via `callbacks_->route()`:\n\n```cpp\n// router.cc:471\nroute_ = callbacks_->route();\nif (!route_) {\n    callbacks_->sendLocalReply(Http::Code::NotFound, ...);\n    return StopIteration;\n}\n```\n\nThe `ActiveStream` implements `RouteCache`. It lazily calls `ConnectionManagerConfig::routeConfigProvider()` (for static/RDS routes) or `scopedRouteConfigProvider()` (for scoped routing), matches the request headers against the `RouteConfiguration`, and caches the result. The route cache is **blocked** (frozen) at the point response headers are processed, preventing route mutations during the response path.\n\nRoute matching is done by `Router::ConfigImpl::route()` (`source/common/router/config_impl.cc`), which walks virtual hosts, then route entries (prefix, path, regex), and evaluates route matchers (headers, query params, runtime fractions).\n\nOnce a route entry is selected:\n- `route_entry_->clusterName()` (or a `ClusterSpecifierPlugin`) identifies the target cluster.\n- `config_->cm_.getThreadLocalCluster(name)` obtains the thread-local cluster object (or null if not found \u2192 503).\n\n### Host Selection and Connection Pool Acquisition\n\nAfter the cluster is identified, the router selects a host and creates a connection pool handle:\n\n```cpp\n// router.cc:700\nauto host_selection_response = cluster->chooseHost(this);\n// ...\nstd::unique_ptr<GenericConnPool> generic_conn_pool = createConnPool(*cluster, selected_host);\n```\n\n`chooseHost()` delegates to the cluster's `LoadBalancer` (inside `ClusterEntry`). If asynchronous host selection is enabled (e.g., on-demand CDS), `chooseHost` returns a cancellable handle and a callback is registered; filter chain iteration returns `StopAllIterationAndWatermark` until the async callback fires.\n\n`createConnPool()` calls `cluster->httpConnPool(host, priority, downstream_protocol, this)`, which returns a `GenericConnPool` wrapping the appropriate `Http::ConnectionPool::Instance`. The connection pool is keyed by (host, priority, protocol) in the thread-local `host_http_conn_pool_map_`.\n\n### UpstreamRequest Lifecycle\n\nFor each attempt (initial + retries), the router creates an `UpstreamRequest`:\n\n```cpp\n// router.cc:842\nUpstreamRequestPtr upstream_request = std::make_unique<UpstreamRequest>(\n    *this, std::move(generic_conn_pool), can_send_early_data, can_use_http3, enable_half_close);\nLinkedList::moveIntoList(std::move(upstream_request), upstream_requests_);\nupstream_requests_.front()->acceptHeadersFromRouter(end_stream);\n```\n\n`UpstreamRequest` owns an **upstream filter chain** via `UpstreamFilterManager` and `UpstreamRequestFilterManagerCallbacks`. Request data arriving via `acceptHeadersFromRouter`, `acceptDataFromRouter`, `acceptTrailersFromRouter` is passed into this upstream filter manager. The last filter in the upstream chain is always `UpstreamCodecFilter` (`source/common/router/upstream_codec_filter.cc`), which holds the actual stream on the upstream connection.\n\nWhen the upstream connection is not yet ready, `UpstreamCodecFilter` returns `StopAllIteration`, causing the upstream filter manager to buffer the request and use watermarks to push back on the router (and in turn the downstream) if buffers fill up.\n\nOn `onPoolReady` (connection established, stream allocated):\n1. The `UpstreamRequest` obtains a `GenericUpstream` handle.\n2. `UpstreamCodecFilter` encodes the buffered request headers/data.\n\nOn `onPoolFailure` (no healthy hosts, connection error, etc.):\n1. `UpstreamRequest::onPoolFailure()` calls `parent_.onUpstreamAbort()`.\n2. The router checks the retry policy; if retriable, it calls `doRetry()`.\n3. If no more retries, `sendLocalReply` is called with a 503 or 504.\n\n### Retry Logic\n\n`RetryStateImpl` (`source/common/router/retry_state_impl.cc`) evaluates whether a response or reset event is retriable:\n- HTTP status codes (5xx, specific codes).\n- Reset reasons (connection failure, refused-stream).\n- Per-try timeouts with hedging.\n\nOn a retriable failure, `doRetry()` creates a new `UpstreamRequest`, either immediately or after the previous one is fully cleaned up. Retry attempt count and headers (`x-envoy-attempt-count`) are updated on the downstream request before each retry.\n\nHedged requests (configured via `hedge_on_per_try_timeout`) keep the original upstream request alive while launching a new one; when either returns a valid response, the winning response is forwarded downstream and the other upstream request is reset.\n\n### Timeout Handling\n\n`FilterUtility::finalTimeout()` computes two timeout values:\n- **Global timeout**: overall deadline for the entire request including retries.\n- **Per-try timeout**: deadline for each individual upstream attempt.\n\nThe global timeout fires via `response_timeout_` (`Event::TimerPtr`), calling `onGlobalTimeout()` \u2192 `sendLocalReply(504)`. Per-try timeout fires via `UpstreamRequest::per_try_timeout_`, calling `onPerTryTimeout()` which triggers a retry if configured.\n\n### Shadow Routing\n\nShadow (traffic mirroring) is evaluated per route and per cluster `shadowPolicies()`. For each active shadow policy, the router copies the request headers, optionally modifies them (cluster name override, weight-based sampling), and sends to the shadow cluster via `config_->shadowWriter().shadow()`, which uses `Http::AsyncClient` so the shadow stream does not affect the downstream response.\n\n---\n\n## 4. Cluster Manager and Upstream Connectivity\n\n**Source**: `source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.h`, `source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.cc`, `source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.h`, `source/common/http/conn_pool_base.h`\n\n### ClusterManagerImpl\n\n`ClusterManagerImpl` is a singleton (one per Envoy server) that maintains the canonical list of active and warming clusters. Each cluster is represented by a `ClusterData` object holding:\n- `Cluster` \u2014 the cluster implementation (static/EDS/DNS/logical DNS/original dst).\n- `ThreadAwareLoadBalancer` \u2014 if present, a thread-aware LB (e.g., ring hash, maglev); otherwise each thread gets its own independent LB.\n\nCluster updates from CDS flow through `addOrUpdateCluster()`, which updates the main-thread state and then posts to each worker thread via `postThreadLocalClusterUpdate()`.\n\n### ThreadLocalClusterManagerImpl\n\nEach worker thread has a `ThreadLocalClusterManagerImpl` (stored in thread-local storage via `ThreadLocal::Slot`). It holds:\n\n```cpp\nabsl::flat_hash_map<std::string, ClusterEntryPtr> thread_local_clusters_;\nabsl::node_hash_map<HostConstSharedPtr, ConnPoolsContainer> host_http_conn_pool_map_;\n```\n\n`ClusterEntry` (inner class of `ThreadLocalClusterManagerImpl`) implements `ThreadLocalCluster` and owns:\n- `PrioritySetImpl priority_set_` \u2014 the local view of healthy/degraded hosts at each priority level.\n- `LoadBalancerPtr lb_` \u2014 the thread-local load balancer instance.\n\n**Lazy cluster inflation**: With the `ClusterInitializationObject` mechanism, worker threads can defer constructing a `ClusterEntry` until the first request arrives for that cluster (`initializeClusterInlineIfExists`). This reduces memory pressure for clusters that are rarely used on a given thread.\n\n### Load Balancing\n\n`ThreadLocalCluster::chooseHost(LoadBalancerContext*)` calls into the `LoadBalancer` interface. The load balancer is provided by a factory from the cluster configuration:\n- **Round Robin**: iterates hosts in the priority set.\n- **Least Request**: selects the host with the fewest active requests.\n- **Ring Hash / Maglev**: consistent hashing using `computeHashKey()` from the `LoadBalancerContext` (router filter computes the hash from request headers or a cookie).\n- **Random**: uniform random selection.\n- **Custom**: via `loadBalancingPolicy` extension (e.g., `peak_ewma` in contrib).\n\nThe router filter implements `LoadBalancerContextBase` to supply:\n- `computeHashKey()` \u2014 from the `HashPolicy` configured on the route or cluster.\n- `metadataMatchCriteria()` \u2014 merged from route, connection, and request metadata for subset load balancing.\n- `shouldSelectAnotherHost()` \u2014 delegates to `RetryStateImpl` to avoid previously-failed hosts on retry.\n- `determinePriorityLoad()` \u2014 adjusts priority weights on retry.\n\n### Connection Pool Mechanics\n\n`ThreadLocalCluster::httpConnPool(host, priority, downstream_protocol, context)` returns an `HttpPoolData` wrapping the appropriate `Http::ConnectionPool::Instance`. Connection pools are stored in `host_http_conn_pool_map_` keyed by a hash of (host, priority, protocol, options).\n\n`HttpConnPoolImplBase` (`source/common/http/conn_pool_base.h`) is the base for HTTP/1.1 and HTTP/2 pools. It builds on `ConnPoolImplBase` (`source/common/conn_pool/conn_pool_base.h`), which maintains:\n- `pending_streams_` \u2014 requests waiting for a connection.\n- `ready_clients_` \u2014 clients with capacity to accept a new stream.\n- `busy_clients_` \u2014 clients at their concurrent stream limit.\n\nWhen `newStream()` is called:\n1. If a ready client exists, the stream is immediately attached.\n2. If the pool can grow (below `max_connections`), a new `CodecClient` is created (one TCP connection per client for HTTP/1.1, one per cluster host for HTTP/2 multiplexed).\n3. Otherwise, the request queues as an `HttpPendingStream`.\n\nWhen a connection becomes ready (TLS handshake complete, HTTP/2 SETTINGS exchanged), pending streams are drained from the queue. Idle pool connections are drained after `idle_timeout` with a configurable grace period.\n\nFor **HTTP/3 (QUIC)**, the `conn_pool_grid.h` (`Http::ConnectivityGrid`) implements Happy Eyeballs between H3 and H1/H2, falling back if QUIC is unavailable.\n\n### Health Checking and Outlier Detection\n\n**Active health checks** (`source/common/upstream/health_checker_impl.cc`) send periodic HTTP/TCP/gRPC probes to each host. The `HealthCheckerImpl` subscribes to each host and calls `setHealthy()/setUnhealthy()` based on probe results. These status changes are propagated through the `PrioritySet` \u2192 `LoadBalancer`, removing unhealthy hosts from the eligible set.\n\n**Outlier detection** (`source/common/upstream/outlier_detection_impl.cc`) monitors request outcomes reported by the router via `updateOutlierDetection()`:\n\n```cpp\n// router.cc - after receiving upstream response\nvoid Filter::updateOutlierDetection(Upstream::Outlier::Result result,\n                                    UpstreamRequest& upstream_request, ...) {\n    ...host->outlierDetector().putResult(result, code);\n}\n```\n\n`DetectorImpl` accumulates per-host failure counters and runs periodic analysis. When a host breaches a configured threshold (consecutive 5xx errors, local origin failures, success rate below cluster average), it is **ejected** for an exponentially-increasing interval (`base_ejection_time * consecutive_ejections`). Ejected hosts are marked `UNHEALTHY` in the host's health flags and excluded by the load balancer.\n\nHealth state is written by the main thread but read by worker threads through the `HostSharedPtr` reference-counted objects, which carry atomic health-flag bitfields updated with appropriate memory ordering.\n\n---\n\n## 5. Complete Data Flow: Request Path\n\n```\nDownstream TCP/TLS connection\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc\nConnectionManagerImpl::onData()       [Network::ReadFilter]\n  \u2514\u2500 createCodec() if first bytes      [lazy, except QUIC]\n  \u2514\u2500 codec_->dispatch(data)            [ServerConnection: H1/H2/H3 parsing]\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc codec calls ServerConnectionCallbacks\nConnectionManagerImpl::newStream()     [allocates ActiveStream]\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc codec calls RequestDecoder (ActiveStream)\nActiveStream::decodeHeaders()\n  \u2514\u2500 validates headers (UHV if enabled)\n  \u2514\u2500 filter_manager_.decodeHeaders()\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc FilterManager iterates decoder_filters_ forward\n[FilterA::decodeHeaders] \u2192 [FilterB::decodeHeaders] \u2192 [Router::Filter::decodeHeaders]\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc Router::Filter\n  \u2514\u2500 callbacks_->route()              [ActiveStream::route() \u2192 RouteConfig match]\n  \u2514\u2500 config_->cm_.getThreadLocalCluster(cluster_name)\n  \u2514\u2500 cluster->chooseHost(this)         [LoadBalancer host selection]\n  \u2514\u2500 cluster->httpConnPool(host, ...)  [Thread-local pool lookup/create]\n  \u2514\u2500 new UpstreamRequest(conn_pool)\n  \u2514\u2500 upstream_request->acceptHeadersFromRouter()\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc UpstreamRequest / UpstreamFilterManager\n  [UpstreamFilterA \u2192 UpstreamCodecFilter]\n  \u2514\u2500 conn_pool->newStream(response_decoder, callbacks)\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc ConnectionPool\n  \u2514\u2500 Existing idle connection? Attach stream immediately.\n     No? \u2192 Create new CodecClient (TCP connect + TLS + ALPN + H2 SETTINGS)\n     Queue as HttpPendingStream if at capacity.\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc onPoolReady (new or existing upstream connection)\n  \u2514\u2500 UpstreamCodecFilter encodes headers onto upstream stream\n  \u2514\u2500 Upstream data flushed\n```\n\n## 6. Complete Data Flow: Response Path\n\n```\nUpstream bytes received by CodecClient\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc UpstreamCodecFilter::CodecBridge (Http::ResponseDecoder)\n  \u2514\u2500 decode1xxHeaders / decodeHeaders / decodeData / decodeTrailers\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc UpstreamRequestFilterManagerCallbacks::encodeHeaders()\n  \u2514\u2500 upstream_request_.decodeHeaders(response_headers, end_stream)\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc UpstreamRequest::decodeHeaders()\n  \u2514\u2500 parent_.onUpstreamHeaders(status_code, headers, upstream_request, end_stream)\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc Router::Filter::onUpstreamHeaders()\n  \u2514\u2500 Check for retry: RetryStateImpl::shouldRetryHeaders()\n     If retry \u2192 doRetry() \u2192 new UpstreamRequest\n     Else \u2192 forward downstream:\n  \u2514\u2500 callbacks_->encodeHeaders(response_headers, end_stream)   [ActiveStreamDecoderFilter]\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc FilterManager::encodeHeaders() \u2014 iterates encoder_filters_ REVERSE\n[Router side-effects] \u2192 [FilterC::encodeHeaders] \u2192 [FilterB::encodeHeaders] \u2192 [FilterA::encodeHeaders]\n        \u2502\n        \u25bc FilterManagerCallbacks::encodeHeaders() [ActiveStream]\n  \u2514\u2500 response_encoder_->encodeHeaders()          [H1/H2/H3 ResponseEncoder]\n  \u2514\u2500 Bytes written to downstream connection write buffer\n  \u2514\u2500 Access logging on stream completion\n  \u2514\u2500 doDeferredStreamDestroy(stream)\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Extension Points\n\n| Extension Point | Interface / Location |\n|---|---|\n| **HTTP filters** (decoder/encoder/dual) | `Http::StreamDecoderFilter`, `Http::StreamEncoderFilter`, `Http::StreamFilter` registered via `NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory` |\n| **Upstream HTTP filters** | Same interfaces, registered via `UpstreamHttpFilterConfigFactory`, placed in `UpstreamFilterManager` |\n| **Load balancers** | `LoadBalancerFactory` / `ThreadAwareLoadBalancerFactory` (`envoy/upstream/load_balancer.h`) |\n| **Cluster types** | `ClusterFactory` (`envoy/upstream/cluster_factory.h`) |\n| **Health checkers** | `HealthCheckerFactory` (`envoy/server/health_checker_config.h`) |\n| **Outlier detectors** | `OutlierDetectionFactory` |\n| **Access loggers** | `AccessLog::InstanceFactory` (`envoy/access_log/access_log_config.h`) |\n| **Tracers** | `Tracing::Driver` factory (`envoy/server/tracer_config.h`) |\n| **Route config providers** | `RouteConfigProviderManager`, `RdsRouteConfigProviderFactory` |\n| **Cluster specifier plugins** | `ClusterSpecifierPlugin` (`envoy/router/cluster_specifier_plugin.h`) |\n| **Request ID extensions** | `RequestIDExtension` (`envoy/http/request_id_extension.h`) |\n| **Header validators** | `HeaderValidatorFactory` (`envoy/http/header_validator_factory.h`) \u2014 compile-time via `ENVOY_ENABLE_UHV` |\n| **Original IP detection** | `OriginalIPDetectionExtension` (`envoy/http/original_ip_detection.h`) |\n| **Early header mutations** | `EarlyHeaderMutation` (`envoy/http/early_header_mutation.h`) |\n| **Shadow writers** | `ShadowWriter` (`envoy/router/shadow_writer.h`) |\n\n---\n\n## 8. Error Handling\n\n### Codec Errors\n\nDetected in `ConnectionManagerImpl::onData()` after `codec_->dispatch()`. The returned `Status` is classified:\n\n- `isBufferFloodError` / `isInboundFramesWithEmptyPayloadError` \u2192 `handleCodecError()` \u2192 `doConnectionClose(FlushWriteAndDelay)`.\n- `isCodecProtocolError` \u2192 same, increments `downstream_cx_protocol_error_`.\n- `isEnvoyOverloadError` \u2192 `handleCodecOverloadError()` \u2192 same.\n\nHTTP/1 codec sends a `400 Bad Request` before closing. HTTP/2 codec sends a GOAWAY. All active streams receive an `onResetStream` callback from `resetAllStreams()`.\n\n### Filter Errors\n\n- A filter returning `StopIteration` during `decodeHeaders` after calling `sendLocalReply` initiates the local reply path. The downstream filter chain iteration is aborted (`decoder_filter_chain_aborted_ = true`). The local reply goes through encoder filters (or is sent directly if encoder chain is not applicable).\n- If a filter throws (fatal error), Envoy's crash handler terminates. Non-fatal filter errors must be handled by the filter itself using `sendLocalReply`.\n- The `MissingConfigFilter` handles the ECDS case where a dynamic filter configuration has not yet loaded, returning a 500.\n\n### Upstream Failures\n\nHandled by `Router::Filter`:\n\n| Failure Type | Handling |\n|---|---|\n| Pool failure (no healthy upstream) | `onPoolFailure()` \u2192 `onUpstreamAbort()` \u2192 retry or 503 |\n| Connection reset during request | `onUpstreamReset()` \u2192 retry if `RetryState::shouldRetryReset()` |\n| Per-try timeout | `onPerTryTimeout()` \u2192 retry with hedging if enabled |\n| Global timeout | `onGlobalTimeout()` \u2192 `sendLocalReply(504)`, all upstream requests reset |\n| Upstream 5xx response | `RetryState::shouldRetryHeaders()` \u2192 retry or forward to downstream |\n| Upstream max stream duration | `onStreamMaxDurationReached()` \u2192 reset upstream, retry or 504 |\n\nUpstream failures are also reported to outlier detection via `updateOutlierDetection()`, contributing to host ejection.\n\n### Connection-Level Failures\n\n`ConnectionManagerImpl::onEvent()` handles `Network::ConnectionEvent::RemoteClose` and `LocalClose`. It calls `resetAllStreams(CoreResponseFlag::DownstreamConnectionTermination, ...)`, which invokes `onResetStream` on every `ActiveStream`, causing the router to clean up upstream connections.\n\n---\n\n## 9. Key Source Files Reference\n\n| Component | File |\n|---|---|\n| HCM implementation | `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h`, `.cc` |\n| HCM configuration | `source/common/http/conn_manager_config.h` |\n| Filter Manager | `source/common/http/filter_manager.h`, `.cc` |\n| Filter chain construction | `source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h`, `.cc` |\n| Router filter | `source/common/router/router.h`, `.cc` |\n| Router config (route matching) | `source/common/router/config_impl.h`, `.cc` |\n| Upstream request | `source/common/router/upstream_request.h`, `.cc` |\n| Upstream codec filter | `source/common/router/upstream_codec_filter.h`, `.cc` |\n| Retry state | `source/common/router/retry_state_impl.h`, `.cc` |\n| Shadow writer | `source/common/router/shadow_writer_impl.h`, `.cc` |\n| Cluster manager | `source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.h`, `.cc` |\n| Cluster implementation | `source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.h`, `.cc` |\n| HTTP connection pool base | `source/common/http/conn_pool_base.h`, `.cc` |\n| HTTP/1 connection pool | `source/common/http/http1/` |\n| HTTP/2 connection pool | `source/common/http/http2/` |\n| H2+H3 grid pool | `source/common/http/conn_pool_grid.h`, `.cc` |\n| Health checker | `source/common/upstream/health_checker_impl.h`, `.cc` |\n| Outlier detection | `source/common/upstream/outlier_detection_impl.h`, `.cc` |\n| Public HCM filter interface | `envoy/http/filter.h` |\n| Cluster manager interface | `envoy/upstream/cluster_manager.h` |\n| Load balancer interface | `envoy/upstream/load_balancer.h` |\n",

# Envoy HTTP Connection Manager: Architecture and Data Flow

## Overview

The HTTP Connection Manager (HCM) is Envoy's central HTTP processing engine. It is a `Network::ReadFilter` that sits inside the listener filter chain and transforms a raw TCP/TLS/QUIC byte stream into structured HTTP request/response lifecycles. Four major subsystems collaborate to service every request:

1. **`ConnectionManagerImpl`** — owns the connection lifecycle and codec, multiplexes raw bytes into per-request `ActiveStream` objects.
2. **`FilterManager` / `DownstreamFilterManager`** — owns per-stream decoder and encoder filter chains, drives filter iteration.
3. **`Router::Filter`** — the terminal decoder filter; owns route selection, upstream connection, retry, and shadow logic.
4. **`ClusterManagerImpl` / `ThreadLocalClusterManagerImpl`** — owns upstream cluster state, load balancing, and connection pools.

---

## 1. ConnectionManagerImpl

**Source**: `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h`, `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.cc`

### Role

`ConnectionManagerImpl` implements three interfaces simultaneously:

- `Network::ReadFilter` — receives raw bytes from the transport layer.
- `Http::ServerConnectionCallbacks` — called by the codec when a new HTTP stream is parsed.
- `Network::ConnectionCallbacks` — receives connection-level events (close, watermarks).

It is instantiated per downstream TCP connection by the HCM network filter factory. The configuration comes from `ConnectionManagerConfig` (`source/common/http/conn_manager_config.h`), which exposes codec factory methods, timeout values, the filter chain factory, route provider, tracer, and access loggers.

### Codec Instantiation (Lazy for H1/H2, Eager for H3)

The codec is created lazily:

- For **HTTP/1 and HTTP/2**, `onData()` 
... (truncated)
